                            <script>
                                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
                                    const valueinput = document.getElementById('setting_time');
                                    const timeinput = document.getElementById('setting_time1');
                                    let actualtimeValue = valueinput.value;
                                    // 
                                    updateValueInputDisplay();
                                    updateTimeInputDisplay();
                                    console.log("actualtimeValue:" ,actualtimeValue)
                                    // valueinput 
                                    valueinput.addEventListener('focus', () => {
                                        valueinput.value = actualtimeValue;
                                    });
                                    // valueinput 
 timeinput
                                    valueinput.addEventListener('blur', () => {
                                        actualtimeValue = valueinput.value.replace(/[^\d]/g, '');
                                        custom_time_value = actualtimeValue
                                        updateValueInputDisplay();
                                        updateTimeInputDisplay();
                                        remainingSeconds = custom_time_value * 60 *60
                                        ws_send_data('settings', {'filament_timer': custom_time_value});
                                    });
                                    function updateValueInputDisplay() {
                                        valueinput.value = actualtimeValue ? `${actualtimeValue}H` : '';
                                    }
                                    function updateTimeInputDisplay() {
                                        // 
 disabled 
                                        // timeinput.value = actualtimeValue ? `${parseInt(actualtimeValue, 10) % 24}:00` : '';
                                        timeinput.value = actualtimeValue ? `${actualtimeValue}:00` : '';
                                    }
                                });
                            </script>

            <script>
                let isRunning = 0; // 
                let countdownInterval = null; // 
                function btn_start_drying_click() {
                    const ele = document.getElementById('id_btn_start_drying');
                    
                    if (!isRunning) {
                        // 
                        isRunning = 1;
                        startCountdown();
                        updateButtonText(ele); // 
                    } else {
                        // 
                        isRunning = 0;
                        pauseCountdown();
                        updateButtonText(ele); // 
                    }
                    ws_send_data('settings', {'isrunning': isRunning});
                }   
                function startCountdown() {
                    if (countdownInterval) clearInterval(countdownInterval);
                    
                    countdownInterval = setInterval(() => {
                        remainingSeconds--;
                        
                        // 
                        if (remainingSeconds <= 0) {
                            remainingSeconds = actualtimeValue * 60 * 60; // 
                            pauseCountdown();
                            isRunning = 0;
                            updateButtonText(document.getElementById('id_btn_start_drying'));
                            alert(g_lang === "en" ? "Drying completed!" : "
                        }
                        
                        // 
                        updateButtonText(document.getElementById('id_btn_start_drying'));
                    }, 1000);
                }
                // 
                function pauseCountdown() {
                    clearInterval(countdownInterval);
                    countdownInterval = null;
                }
                // 
HH:MM
                function formatTime(seconds) {
                    const hours = Math.floor(seconds / 3600);
                    const minutes = Math.floor((seconds % 3600) / 60);
                    return `${hours.toString().padStart(2, '0')}:${minutes.toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
                }
                // 
                function updateButtonText(ele) {
                    const timeStr = formatTime(remainingSeconds);
                    const timeinput1 = document.getElementById('setting_time1');
                    timeinput1.value = timeStr
                    if (isRunning) {
                        // 
                        ele.textContent = g_lang === "en" 
                            ? `Pause Drying` 
                            : `
                    } else {
                        // 
                        ele.textContent = g_lang === "en" 
                            ? `Start Drying` 
                            : `
                    }
                }
                // 
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
                    updateButtonText(document.getElementById('setting_time1'));
                });
            </script>   
            <script>
                const modeSwitch = document.getElementById('modeSwitch');
                const autoModeButton = document.getElementById('autoMode');
                const powerOnModeButton = document.getElementById('powerOnMode');
                const filamentDryingModeButton = document.getElementById('filamentDryingMode');
                const functionmodules = document.getElementById('functionmodules');
                const functionmodules1 = document.getElementById('functionmodules1');
                const functionmodules2 = document.getElementById('functionmodules2');
                   
                autoModeButton.classList.add('active');
                functionmodules.classList.add('active'); 
                functionmodules1.classList.add('active');
                autoModeButton.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    removeActiveClass();
                    this.classList.add('active');
                    functionmodules.classList.add('active');
                    functionmodules1.classList.add('active');
                    functionmodules2.classList.remove('active');
                    ws_send_data('settings', {'work_mode': 3});
                });
                powerOnModeButton.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    removeActiveClass();
                    this.classList.add('active');
                    functionmodules.classList.add('active');
                    functionmodules1.classList.remove('active');
                    functionmodules2.classList.remove('active');
                    ws_send_data('settings', {'work_mode': 2});
                });
                filamentDryingModeButton.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    removeActiveClass();
                    this.classList.add('active');
                    functionmodules.classList.remove('active');
                    functionmodules1.classList.remove('active');
                    functionmodules2.classList.add('active');
                    ws_send_data('settings', {'work_mode': 1});
                });
                function removeActiveClass() {
                const modeButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.work_mode_item');
                modeButtons.forEach(function (button) {
                    button.classList.remove('active');
                });
                }
            </script>

        let g_hello_running = true;
        const g_hello_texts = ["Hello", "
", "Bonjour", "Hola", "Ol
", "
", "
        let g_hello_text_index = 0;
        const g_hello_group = document.getElementById('group_hello_path');
        let g_hello_offset_y = 0;
        let g_hello_direction = 1;
        function hello_animate_path() {
            g_hello_offset_y += g_hello_direction;
            if (g_hello_offset_y >= 10) {
                g_hello_direction = -1;
            }
            if (g_hello_offset_y < 0) {
                g_hello_offset_y = 0;
                g_hello_direction = 1;
                return;
            }
            const currentTransform = g_hello_group.transform.baseVal.getItem(0);
            const matrix = currentTransform.matrix;
            currentTransform.setTranslate(matrix.e, 50 + g_hello_offset_y);
            requestAnimationFrame(hello_animate_path);
        }
        function hello_change_text() {
            const textElement = document.getElementById('id_text_hello');
            textElement.textContent = g_hello_texts[g_hello_text_index];
            g_hello_text_index = (g_hello_text_index + 1) % g_hello_texts.length;
        }
        function hello_frame() {
            if (!g_hello_running) return;
            hello_animate_path();
            setTimeout(hello_change_text, 100);
        }
        function hello_visibility_change() {
            if (document.visibilityState === 'hidden') {
                g_hello_running = false;
            } else if (document.visibilityState === 'visible') {
                g_hello_running = true;
            }
        }
        function load_img() {
            document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', hello_visibility_change, false);
            hello_change_text();
            setInterval(hello_frame, 1700);
            document.getElementById("id_img_scan_wifi").src = base64_scan;
            document.getElementById("id_img_scan_printer").src = base64_scan;

        }
        function format_string(str, ...args) {
            let index = 0;
            return str.replace(/%[^%]/g, (m) => {
                if (index >= args.length)
                    return m;
                const arg = args[index++];
                return String(arg);
            });
        }
        function language_navigate(lang) {
            g_lang = lang;
            const id_btn_lang = "id_btn_language_" + g_lang;
            document.getElementById("id_settings_lang").value = g_lang;
            document.querySelectorAll('[id^="id_btn_language_"]').forEach(btn => {
                btn.classList.add('cancel');
            });
            let btn_element = document.getElementById(id_btn_lang);
            if (btn_element) {
                btn_element.classList.remove('cancel');
            }
            document.querySelectorAll('[data-translate]').forEach(context => {
                const key = context.getAttribute('data-translate');
                if (key !== '') {
                    // const text_str = g_lang_resources[key] ? g_lang_resources[key][g_lang] : key;
                    const text_str = g_lang_resources[key][g_lang];
                    const arg = context.getAttribute('data-arg');
                    const text = format_string(text_str, arg);
                    context.innerHTML = format_string(text_str, arg);
                    if (key.startsWith("placeholder_")) {
                        context.setAttribute("placeholder", text);
                    } else {
                        context.innerHTML = text;
                    }
                }
            });
        }
        function page_navigate(id) {
            let id_page = "id_page_" + id;
            document.querySelectorAll('.c_page').forEach(page => {
                page.classList.remove('active');
            });
            let page_element = document.getElementById(id_page);
            if (page_element) {
                page_element.classList.add('active');
            }
        }
        function card_navigate(id) {
            let id_btn = "id_btn_" + id;
            let id_card = "id_card_" + id;
            document.querySelectorAll('.c_card_ctl button').forEach(btn =>{
                btn.classList.remove('active');
            });
            let btn_element = document.getElementById(id_btn);
            if (btn_element) {
                btn_element.classList.add('active');
            }
            document.querySelectorAll('.c_card').forEach(card => {
                card.classList.remove('active');
            });
            let card_element = document.getElementById(id_card);
            if (card_element) {
                card_element.classList.add('active');
            }
            if (id !== 'theme') {
                // preview_ui_switch(false);
            }
        }
        function dialog_create(key_title, key_text, btns) {
            let dialog = document.getElementById("id_dialog");
            dialog.classList.add('active');
            let ele_title = document.getElementById("id_dialog_title");
            let ele_text = document.getElementById("id_dialog_text");
            ele_title.innerHTML = g_lang_resources[key_title] ? g_lang_resources[key_title][g_lang] : key_title;
            ele_text.innerHTML = g_lang_resources[key_text] ? g_lang_resources[key_text][g_lang] : key_text;
            let ele_btn = document.getElementById("id_dialog_btn");
            // clean btns
            while (ele_btn.firstChild) {
                ele_btn.removeChild(ele_btn.firstChild);
            }
            // Set btns
            btns.forEach(btn => {
                let b = document.createElement("button");
                b.innerText = g_lang_resources[btn.key] ? g_lang_resources[btn.key][g_lang] : btn.key;
                b.classList.add("c_btn_submit");
                if (btn.key === 'cancel') {
                    b.classList.add("cancel");
                }
                b.onclick = function() {
                    if (btn.handler != null) {
                        btn.handler();
                    }
                    dialog_close();
                };
                ele_btn.appendChild(b);
            });
        }
        function dialog_close() {
            let dialog = document.getElementById("id_dialog");
            dialog.classList.remove('active');
        }
        function show_note_sta_ip() {

        function html_require_refresh() {
            location.href = location.href;
        }
        function ota_btn_disable(id, disable) {
            let btn_ele= document.getElementById('id_btn_' + id);
            btn_ele.disabled = disable;
            btn_ele.classList.toggle('readonly', disable);
        }
        const g_ota_id = ['ota_fw'];
        function ota_btns_disable(disable) {            
            for (let i = 0; i < g_ota_id.length; i++) {
                ota_btn_disable(g_ota_id[i], disable)
            }
        }
        function ota_status_change(id, start) {
            const btn_ele = document.getElementById('id_btn_' + id);
            const status_ele = document.getElementById('id_span_status_' + id);
            const progress_ele = document.getElementById('id_span_progress_' + id);
            const svg_ele = document.getElementById('id_svg_upload_' + id);
            ota_btns_disable(start);
            if (status_ele) {
                // updating
                const text_ok = 'ota_info_' + id;
                const text_start = 'updating';
                status_ele.dataset.translate = start ? text_start : text_ok;
                status_ele.innerHTML = g_lang_resources[status_ele.dataset.translate][g_lang];
            }
            if (progress_ele) {
                progress_ele.innerHTML = start ? '(0%)' : '';
            }
            if (svg_ele) {
                svg_ele.classList.toggle('ele_hidden', start);
            }
            if (btn_ele) {
                btn_ele.classList.toggle('progress', start);
            }
        }
        function ota_post_file(file, id) {
            let post_path = "ota";
            ota_status_change(id, 1);
            let xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
            xhr.open("POST", post_path, true);
            xhr.setRequestHeader("Content-Type", "application/octet-stream;charset=UTF-8");
            xhr.setRequestHeader('OTA-Type', id); 
            xhr.upload.addEventListener("progress",
                function(post_path) {
                    let progress_ele= document.getElementById("id_span_progress_" + id);
                    let progress = Math.floor(post_path.loaded * 100 / post_path.total);
                    progress_ele.innerHTML = "(" + progress + "%)";
                }
            );
            xhr.send(file);
        }
        function ota_file_selected(f_type, id, max_size) {
            let file = event.target.files[0];
            if (!file) return;
            let file_max_size = parseInt(max_size);
            if (file.size > file_max_size) {
                const f_size = (file.size / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2);
                const fm_size = (file_max_size / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2);
                const f_size_error = {
                    en: `file size is: ${f_size}MB, should not exceed: ${fm_size}MB`,
                    zh: `
${f_size}MB, 
: ${fm_size}MB`,
                };
                dialog_create(file.name, f_size_error[g_lang], [{key: 'note_ok', handler: null}]);
                return ;
            }
            if (f_type !== '.gif') {
                ota_post_file(file, id);
                return;
            }
        }
        function ota_btn_click(f_type, id, max_size) {
            let input_ele = document.getElementById('id_file_input');
            input_ele.accept = f_type;
            input_ele.onchange = function() {
                ota_file_selected(f_type, id, max_size);
            }
            input_ele.click();
            input_ele.value = null;
        }

            language_set_by_id(select.value)
        }
        const g_printing_ui_type_str = ['progress', 'gif', 'progress_gif'];

        // WebSocket
        let g_websocket;
        function ws_init(event) {
            console.log('Trying to open a WebSocket connection
            let gateway = `ws://${window.location.host}/ws`;
            g_websocket = new WebSocket(gateway);
            g_websocket.onopen = ws_on_open;
            g_websocket.onclose = ws_on_close;
            g_websocket.onmessage = ws_on_message;
        }
        function ws_on_open(event) {
            console.log('Connection opened');
        }
        function ws_on_close(event) {
            console.log('Connection closed');
            show_ws_not_open();
        }
        function select_add_option(select, value, text) {
            if (!select.querySelector('option[value="' + value + '"]')) {
                let newOption = new Option(text, value);
                select.add(newOption);
            }
        }
        const g_second_timer = {
            wifi_scan: {timer: null, cnt: 0},
            printer_scan: {timer: null, cnt: 0},
            printer_bind: {timer: null, cnt: 0}
        };
        function scan_start_timer(ele, timer) {
            if (timer['timer'] !== null) return;
            timer['cnt'] = 1;
            ele.innerHTML = timer['cnt'];
            timer['timer'] = setInterval(
                function() {
                    timer['cnt']++;
                    ele.innerHTML = timer['cnt'];
                }, 1000);
        }
        function scan_stop_timer(timer) {
            if (timer['timer'] === null) return;
            clearInterval(timer['timer']);
            timer['timer'] = null;
        }
        function btn_scan_remove_rotating(id) {
            let img = document.getElementById("id_img_scan_" + id);
            let span = document.getElementById("id_span_scan_" + id);
            let timer_id = id + "_scan";
            img.classList.remove('c_img_spinning');
            scan_stop_timer(g_second_timer[timer_id]);
            span.dataset.translate = "scan";
            span.innerHTML = g_lang_resources[span.dataset.translate][g_lang];
        }
        function btn_scan_add_rotating(id) {
            let img = document.getElementById("id_img_scan_" + id);
            let span = document.getElementById("id_span_scan_" + id);
            let timer_id = id + "_scan";
            img.classList.add('c_img_spinning');
            span.dataset.translate = "";
            scan_start_timer(span, g_second_timer[timer_id]);
        }
        let g_printer_now = {};
        let g_printer_list = [];
        function printer_clear(printer) {
            g_printer_list.length = 0 ;
        }
        function printer_add_member(printer) {
            let e = g_printer_list.find(d => d.sn === printer.sn);
            if (!e) {
                g_printer_list.push(printer);
            } else {
                if ((e.access_code === '') && (printer.access_code !== '')) {
                    e.access_code = printer.access_code;
                }
            }
        }
        function printer_select_change(select) {
            let e = g_printer_list.find(d => d.sn === select.value);
            if (e) {
                document.getElementById('id_printer_sn').value = e.sn;
                document.getElementById('id_printer_access_code').value = e.access_code;
                document.getElementById('id_printer_ip').value = e.ip;
            }
        }
        let g_wifi_now = {};
        function ws_on_message(event) {
            // console.log("ws_on_message: ", event.data);
            let data = JSON.parse(event.data);
            // wifi
            if (data.wifi !== undefined) {
                let wifi = data.wifi;
                if (wifi.ssid !== undefined) {
                    let ssid = wifi.ssid;
                    if (ssid != '') {
                        let password = ''
                        if (wifi.password !== undefined) {
                            password = wifi.password;
                            document.getElementById("id_password_wifi").value = password;
                        }
                        let select = document.getElementById("id_wifi_ssid");
                        select_add_option(select, ssid, ssid)
                        select.value = ssid;
                        g_wifi_now = {
                            ssid: ssid,
                            password: password
                        };
                    } else {
                        page_navigate('language');
                    }
                }
                if (wifi.scan !== undefined) {
                    scan = wifi.scan;
                    // 0: idle, 1: scanning, 2: done
                    if (scan == 1) {
                        btn_scan_add_rotating('wifi');
                    } else if (scan == 2) {
                        if (g_second_timer['wifi_scan']['timer'] !== null) {
                            btn_scan_remove_rotating('wifi');
                            dialog_create('response_title', 'wifi_scan_ok', [{key: 'note_ok', handler: null}]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                if (wifi.list !== undefined) {
                    const list = wifi.list;
                    const select = document.getElementById("id_wifi_ssid");
                    const password = document.getElementById("id_password_wifi");
                    select.length = 0;// clear select option
                    password.value = '';
                    for (let i = 0; i < list.length; i++) {
                        if (list[i]["ssid"] == '') continue;
                        const ssid = list[i]["ssid"];
                        select_add_option(select, ssid, ssid)
                    }
                    select.value = '';
                    if (g_wifi_now['ssid'] != undefined) {
                        select_add_option(select, g_wifi_now['ssid'], g_wifi_now['ssid']);
                        select.value = g_wifi_now['ssid'];
                        password.value = g_wifi_now['password'];
                    }
                }
            }
            // sta
            if (data.sta !== undefined) {
                let sta = data.sta;
                if (sta.ip !== undefined) {
                    let ip = sta.ip;
                    document.getElementById("id_sta_ip").value = ip;
                }
                if (sta.hostname !== undefined) {
                    let hostname = sta.hostname;
                    document.getElementById("id_sta_hostname").value = hostname;
                }
                if (sta.state !== undefined) {
                    let state = sta.state;
                    wifi_sta_connect_state(state);
                }
            }
            // ap
            if (data.ap !== undefined) {
                const ap = data.ap;
                if (ap.ssid !== undefined) {
                    const ssid = ap.ssid;
                    document.getElementById("id_ap_ssid").value = ssid;
                }
                if (ap.password !== undefined) {
                    const password = ap.password;
                    document.getElementById("id_password_ap").value = password;
                }
                if (ap.ip !== undefined) {
                    const ip = ap.ip;
                    document.getElementById("id_ap_ip").value = ip;
                }
                if (ap.on !== undefined) {
                    const on = ap.on;
                    ap_ui_switch(on);
                }
            }
            // printer
            if (data.printer !== undefined) {
                let printer = data.printer;
                if (printer.name !== undefined) {
                    let name = printer.name;
                    let sn = printer.sn;
                    let access_code = printer.access_code;
                    let ip = printer.ip;
                    if (name != '') {
                        document.getElementById("id_printer_sn").value = sn;
                        document.getElementById("id_printer_access_code").value = access_code;
                        document.getElementById("id_printer_ip").value = ip;
                        let select = document.getElementById("id_printer_name");
                        select_add_option(select, sn, name)
                        select.value = sn;
                        g_printer_now = {
                            name: name,
                            sn: sn,
                            access_code: access_code,
                            ip: ip
                        };
                        printer_add_member(g_printer_now);
                    }
                }
                if (printer.state !== undefined) {
                    state = printer.state;
                    btn_printer_set_state(state)
                }
                if (printer.scan !== undefined) {
                    scan = printer.scan;
                    let scanning = 0
                    let key_title = '';
                    let key_text = '';
                    let btns = [{key: 'note_ok', handler: null}];
                    // 0: idle, 1: scanning, 2: done
                    // 3: ip_change_scanning, 4: sn not matched, 5: ip not changed, 6: new ip applied
                    switch(scan) {
                        case 1:
                        case 3:
                            scanning = 1;
                            break;
                        case 2:
                            scanning = 0
                            key_title = 'response_title';
                            key_text = 'printer_scan_ok';
                            break;
                        case 4:
                            scanning = 0
                            key_title = 'note_title';
                            key_text = 'note_bind_ip_change_sn_not_matched';
                            break;
                        case 5:
                            scanning = 0
                            key_title = 'note_title';
                            key_text = 'note_bind_ip_change_ip_not_changed';
                            btns = [
                                {
                                    key: 'go_to_ap',
                                    handler: function() {
                                        card_navigate('ap')
                                    }
                                }, {
                                    key: 'cancel',
                                    handler: null
                                }
                            ];
                            break;
                        case 6:
                            scanning = 0
                            key_title = 'note_title';
                            key_text = 'note_bind_ip_change_new_ip_applied';
                            break;
                    }
                    if (scanning) {
                        btn_scan_add_rotating('printer');
                    } else {
                        if (g_second_timer['printer_scan']['timer'] !== null) {
                            btn_scan_remove_rotating('printer');
                            dialog_create(key_title, key_text, btns);
                        }
                    }
                }
                if (printer.list !== undefined) {
                    let list = printer.list;
                    printer_clear();
                    let select = document.getElementById("id_printer_name");
                    select.length = 0; // clear select option
                    document.getElementById('id_printer_sn').value = "";
                    document.getElementById('id_printer_access_code').value = "";
                    document.getElementById('id_printer_ip').value = "";
                    for (let i = 0; i < list.length; i++) {
                        let name = list[i]["name"];
                        let sn = list[i]["sn"];
                        let ip = list[i]["ip"];
                        let access_code = list[i]["access_code"];
                        select_add_option(select, sn, name)
                        printer_add_member(list[i]);
                    }
                    select.value = '';
                    if (g_printer_now['sn'] != undefined) {
                        select_add_option(select, g_printer_now['sn'], g_printer_now['name']);
                        printer_add_member(g_printer_now);
                        select.value = g_printer_now["sn"];
                        printer_select_change(select);
                    }
                }
            }
            // settings
            if (data.settings !== undefined) {
                const settings = data.settings;
                if (settings.img_version !== undefined) {
                    const img_version = settings.img_version;
                    document.getElementById("id_settings_img_ver").value = img_version;
                }
                if (settings.fw_version !== undefined) {
                    const fw_version = settings.fw_version;
                    document.getElementById("id_settings_fw_ver").value = fw_version;
                }
                if (settings.language !== undefined) {
                    const language = settings.language;
                    language_navigate(language);
                }
                if (settings.printing_ui_type !== undefined) {
                    const printing_ui_type = parseInt(settings.printing_ui_type);
                    const select = document.getElementById("id_settings_printing_ui_type");
                    select.value = g_printing_ui_type_str[printing_ui_type];
                }
                if(settings.work_on !== undefined) {
                    const work_on = settings.work_on;
                    panda_breath_work_on_switch(work_on);
                }
                if(settings.work_mode !== undefined) {
                    const work_mode = settings.work_mode;
                    panda_breath_current_mode_switch(work_mode);
                }
                if(settings.temp !== undefined) {
                    const temp = settings.temp;
                    panda_breath_settings_temp(temp);
                }
                if(settings.hotbedtemp !== undefined) {
                    const hotbedtemp = settings.hotbedtemp;
                    panda_breath_settings_hotbedtemp(hotbedtemp);
                }
                if(settings.custom_temp !== undefined) {
                    const custom_temp = settings.custom_temp;
                    panda_breath_settings_custom_temp(custom_temp);
                }
                if(settings.custom_timer !== undefined) {
                    const custom_timer = settings.custom_timer;
                    panda_breath_settings_custom_timer(custom_timer);
                }
                if(settings.warehouse_temper !== undefined) {
                    const warehouse_temper = settings.warehouse_temper;
                    panda_breath_warehouse_temper(warehouse_temper);
                }
            }
            // settings
            if (data.ws_theme !== undefined) {
                const ws_theme = data.ws_theme;
                if (ws_theme.preview !== undefined) {
                    const preview = ws_theme.preview;
                    preview_ui_switch(preview ? true : false);
                    if (preview) {
                        card_navigate('theme');
                    }
                }
            }
            // response
            if (data.response !== undefined) {
                const response = data.response;
                if ((response.type !== undefined) && (response.ok !== undefined)) {
                    const type = response.type;
                    let ok = response.ok;
                    let key_title = '', key_text = '';
                    let dialog_handler = null;
                    const resp = ['set_hostname', 'set_ap', 'set_hotspot_ip', 'factory_reset'];
                    const ota = ['ota_fw', 'ota_img'];
                    if (resp.includes(type)) {
                        key_title = 'response_title';
                        if (ok) {
                            key_text = type + '_ok';
                            if ('set_hostname' === type) {
                                dialog_handler = device_req_restart;
                            } else if ('set_hotspot_ip' === type) {
                                dialog_handler = device_req_restart;
                            }
                        } else {
                            key_text = 'response_err';
                        }
                    } else if (ota.includes(type)) {
                        if (ok) {
                            key_title = 'note_ota_ok';
                            key_text = 'note_' + type + '_ok';
                            if ('ota_fw' === type) {
                                dialog_handler = html_require_refresh;
                            }
                        } else {
                            key_title = 'note_ota_err';
                            key_text = 'note_ota_err';
                        }
                        ota_status_change(type, 0);
                    } else if (type == "ota_unknown") {
                        key_title = 'note_ota_unknown';
                        key_text = 'note_ota_unknown';
                    } else if (type == "ota_get_img") {
                        if (ok) {
                            key_title = 'note_ota_get_ok';
                            key_text = 'note_ota_get_ok';
                        }
                        ota_status_change('ota_get_img', 0);
                    }
                    if ((key_title !== '') && (key_text !== '')) {
                        dialog_create(key_title, key_text, [{key: 'note_ok', handler: dialog_handler}]);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        function show_ws_not_open() {
            dialog_create('note_title', 'ws_not_open', [{key: 'note_ok', handler: html_require_refresh}]);
        }
        function ws_send_json(json) {
            // console.log(`Sending json: ${json}`);
            if (g_websocket.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
                g_websocket.send(json);
            } else {
                console.log("WebSocket is not open, cannot send json.");
                show_ws_not_open();
            }
        }
        function ws_send_data(root, members) {
            let j_obj = {};
            j_obj[root] = {};
            for (const key in members) {
                j_obj[root][key] = members[key];
            }
            const json = JSON.stringify(j_obj);
            ws_send_json(json)
        }
        function device_req_restart() {
            ws_send_data('settings', {'reset': 1});
        }
        function btn_password_click(id) {
            const input = document.getElementById('id_password_' + id);
            const img = document.getElementById('id_img_password_' + id);
            if (input.type === "password") {
                input.type = "text";
                img.classList.add('filter');
            } else {
                input.type = "password";
                img.classList.remove('filter');
            }
        }
        function btn_wifi_scan_click() {
            btn_scan_add_rotating('wifi');
            ws_send_data('wifi', {'scan': 1});
        }
        let g_page_backup = '';
        function page_navigate_wifi_from(backup_page) {
            g_page_backup = backup_page;
            page_navigate('wifi');
            let select = document.getElementById("id_wifi_ssid");
            if (select.length == 0) {
                btn_wifi_scan_click();
            }
        }
        function page_navigate_wifi_back() {
            page_navigate(g_page_backup)
        }
        function btn_printer_scan_click() {
            btn_scan_add_rotating('printer');
            ws_send_data('printer', {'scan': 1});
        }
        function btn_wifi_connect_click() {
            let select = document.getElementById("id_wifi_ssid");
            if (select.selectedIndex < 0) {
                console.log("wifi have not list");
                return;
            }
            let ssid = select.options[select.selectedIndex].text;
            // let password = document.getElementById("id_wifi_password").value;
            let password = document.getElementById("id_password_wifi").value;
            ws_send_data('wifi', {'ssid': ssid, 'password': password});
            page_navigate('app');
        }
        function wifi_sta_connect_state(state) {
            // state 1: nossid, 2: connecting, 3: connected, 4: reconnecting, 5: password error
            let label = document.getElementById("id_label_sta_state");
            switch(state) {
                case 1:
                    // never here
                    label.dataset.translate = "sta_wifi_invalid_info";
                    break;
                case 2:
                    label.dataset.translate = 'sta_wifi_connecting';
                    break;
                case 3:
                    if ((label.dataset.translate === 'sta_wifi_connecting') || (label.dataset.translate === 'sta_wifi_reconnecting')) {
                        dialog_create(
                            'sta_wifi_connection_ok', 'note_sta_wifi_connection_ok', [
                                {
                                    key: 'go_to_printer',
                                    handler: function() {
                                        card_navigate('printer')
                                    }
                                }, {
                                    key: 'cancel',
                                    handler: null
                                }
                            ]
                        )
                    }
                    label.dataset.translate = 'sta_wifi_connection_ok';
                    break;
                case 4:
                    label.dataset.translate = 'sta_wifi_reconnecting';
                    dialog_create('sta_wifi_connection_err', 'sta_wifi_reconnecting', [{key: 'note_ok', handler: null}]);
                    break;
                case 5:
                    label.dataset.translate = 'sta_wifi_password_err';
                    dialog_create('sta_wifi_connection_err', 'sta_wifi_password_err', [{key: 'note_ok', handler: null}]);
                    break;
            }
            label.innerHTML = g_lang_resources[label.dataset.translate][g_lang];
        }
        function btn_sta_set_hostname_click() {
            let hostname = document.getElementById("id_sta_hostname").value;
            ws_send_data('sta', {'hostname': hostname});
        }
        function ap_ui_switch(on) {
            let btn = document.getElementById("id_btn_ap_on");
            let card = document.getElementById("id_card_ap_switch");
            let note = document.getElementById("id_label_ap_note");
            btn.checked = on;
            card.classList.toggle('active', on);
            note.dataset.translate = on ? 'ap_info_on' : 'ap_info_off';
            note.innerHTML = g_lang_resources[note.dataset.translate][g_lang];
        }
        function checkbox_ap_clicked() {
            let ele = document.getElementById('id_btn_ap_on');
            if (ele.checked) {
                dialog_create(
                    'confirm', 'ap_off_confirm', [
                        {
                            key: 'confirm',
                            handler: function() {
                                ele.checked = 0;
                                ap_ui_switch(0);
                                ws_send_data('ap', {'on': 0});
                            }
                        }, {
                            key: 'cancel',
                            handler: null
                        }
                    ]
                )
            } else {
                ele.checked = 1;
                ap_ui_switch(1);
                ws_send_data('ap', {'on': 1});
            }
        }
        function btn_ap_confirm_click() {
            dialog_create(
                'confirm', 'ap_change_confirm', [

                        key: 'confirm',

        function btn_printer_bind_click() {
            let span = document.getElementById("id_span_printer_bind");
            if (span.dataset.translate === 'bind') {
                btn_printer_set_state(2);
                let name = 'manual';
                let select = document.getElementById("id_printer_name");
                if (select.selectedIndex >= 0) {
                    console.log("printer have not list");
                    name = select.options[select.selectedIndex].text;
                }
                let sn = document.getElementById("id_printer_sn").value;;
                let access_code = document.getElementById("id_printer_access_code").value;;
                let ip = document.getElementById("id_printer_ip").value;
                ws_send_data('printer', {'name': name, 'sn': sn, 'access_code': access_code, 'ip': ip});
            } else {
                dialog_create(
                    'confirm', 'note_unbind_info', [
                        {
                            key: 'confirm',
                            handler: function() {
                                btn_printer_set_state(1);
                                ws_send_data('printer', {'disconnect': 1});
                            }
                        }, {
                            key: 'cancel',
                            handler: null
                        }
                    ]
                )
            }
        }
        function btn_printer_disable(disable) {
            let name = document.getElementById("id_printer_name");
            let sn = document.getElementById("id_printer_sn");
            let access_code = document.getElementById("id_printer_access_code");
            let ip = document.getElementById("id_printer_ip");
            let style = disable ? "c_readonly" : "";
            name.disabled = disable;
            sn.disabled = disable;
            access_code.disabled = disable;
            ip.disabled = disable;
            name.className = style;
            sn.className = style;
            access_code.className = style;
            ip.className = style;
        }
        function btn_printer_set_state(state) {
            // state 1: invalid info, 2: connecting, 3: connected, 4: ip err, 5: sn err, 6: access code, 7: unknown err
            let btn = document.getElementById("id_btn_printer_bind");
            let img = document.getElementById("id_img_printer_bind");
            let timer = document.getElementById("id_timer_printer_bind");
            let span = document.getElementById("id_span_printer_bind");
            let disable = 0;
            let key_title = '';
            let key_text = '';
            switch (state) {
                case 0:
                case 1:
                    disable = 0;
                    span.dataset.translate = "bind";
                    break;
                case 2:
                    disable = 1;
                    span.dataset.translate = "binding";
                    break;
                case 3:
                    disable = 1;
                    if (span.dataset.translate === 'binding') {
                        key_title = 'note_title_bind_ok';
                        key_text = 'note_bind_ok';
                    }
                    span.dataset.translate = "unbind";
                    break;
                case 4:
                    key_title = 'note_title_bind_err';
                    key_text = 'note_bind_ip_err';
                    span.dataset.translate = "bind";
                    break;
                case 5:
                    key_title = 'note_title_bind_err';
                    key_text = 'note_bind_sn_err';
                    span.dataset.translate = "bind";
                    break;
                case 6:
                    key_title = 'note_title_bind_err';
                    key_text = 'note_bind_access_code_err';
                    span.dataset.translate = "bind";
                    break;
                case 7:
                    key_title = 'note_title_bind_err';
                    key_text = 'note_bind_unknow_err';
                    span.dataset.translate = "bind";
                    break;
            }
            span.innerHTML = g_lang_resources[span.dataset.translate][g_lang];
            if (span.dataset.translate === 'bind') {
                btn.className = "c_btn_submit";
                img.src = base64_bind;
                scan_stop_timer(g_second_timer['printer_bind']);
                img.classList.remove('c_img_spinning');
                timer.innerHTML = '';
            } else if (span.dataset.translate === 'binding') {
                btn.className = "c_btn_submit cancel"
                img.src = base64_scan;
                img.classList.add('c_img_spinning');
                scan_start_timer(timer, g_second_timer['printer_bind']);
            } else if (span.dataset.translate === 'unbind') {
                btn.className = "c_btn_submit recovery"
                img.src = base64_unbind;
                scan_stop_timer(g_second_timer['printer_bind']);
                img.classList.remove('c_img_spinning');
                timer.innerHTML = '';
            }
            btn_printer_disable(disable);
            if ((key_title !== '') && (key_text !== '')) {
                dialog_create(key_title, key_text, [{key: 'note_ok', handler: null}]);
            }
        }
